\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00173}00173\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{def\ }\_partial\_roc(y\_true,\ y\_predict,\ max\_fpr):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00174}00174\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ fpr,\ tpr,\ \_\ =\ roc\_curve(y\_true,\ y\_predict)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00175}00175\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ new\_fpr\ =\ fpr[fpr\ <=\ max\_fpr]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00176}00176\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ new\_fpr\ =\ np.append(new\_fpr,\ max\_fpr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00177}00177\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ new\_tpr\ =\ tpr[fpr\ <=\ max\_fpr]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00178}00178\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ idx\_out\ =\ np.argmax(fpr\ >\ max\_fpr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00179}00179\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ idx\_in\ =\ idx\_out\ -\/\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00180}00180\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\_interp\ =\ [fpr[idx\_in],\ fpr[idx\_out]]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00181}00181\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\_interp\ =\ [tpr[idx\_in],\ tpr[idx\_out]]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00182}00182\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ new\_tpr\ =\ np.append(new\_tpr,\ np.interp(max\_fpr,\ x\_interp,\ y\_interp))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00183}00183\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ (new\_fpr,\ new\_tpr)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00191}00191\ \ \ \ \ min\_area\ =\ 0.5\ *\ (fpr2\ -\/\ fpr1)\ *\ (fpr2\ +\ fpr1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00192}00192\ \ \ \ \ max\_area\ =\ fpr2\ -\/\ fpr1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l00193}00193\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 0.5\ *\ (1\ +\ (partial\_auc\ -\/\ min\_area)\ /\ (max\_area\ -\/\ min\_area))}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01546}01546\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}"{}"{}Simple\ implementation\ of\ label\ ranking\ average\ precision"{}"{}"{}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01551}01551\ \ \ \ \ score\ =\ np.empty((n\_samples,))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01552}01552\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ i\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ range(n\_samples):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01553}01553\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ The\ best\ rank\ correspond\ to\ 1.\ Rank\ higher\ than\ 1\ are\ worse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01554}01554\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ The\ best\ inverse\ ranking\ correspond\ to\ n\_labels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01555}01555\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ unique\_rank,\ inv\_rank\ =\ np.unique(y\_score[i],\ return\_inverse=\textcolor{keyword}{True})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01556}01556\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_ranks\ =\ unique\_rank.size}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01557}01557\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ rank\ =\ n\_ranks\ -\/\ inv\_rank}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01558}01558\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01559}01559\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ Rank\ need\ to\ be\ corrected\ to\ take\ into\ account\ ties}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01560}01560\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ ex:\ rank\ 1\ ex\ aequo\ means\ that\ both\ label\ are\ rank\ 2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01561}01561\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ corr\_rank\ =\ np.bincount(rank,\ minlength=n\_ranks\ +\ 1).cumsum()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01562}01562\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ rank\ =\ corr\_rank[rank]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01563}01563\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01564}01564\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ relevant\ =\ y\_true[i].nonzero()[0]}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01567}01567\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01571}01571\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ Let's\ count\ the\ number\ of\ relevant\ label\ with\ better\ rank}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01572}01572\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ (smaller\ rank).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01573}01573\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_ranked\_above\ =\ sum(rank[r]\ <=\ rank[label]\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ r\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ relevant)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01574}01574\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ranking_8py_source_l01576}01576\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ score[i]\ +=\ n\_ranked\_above\ /\ rank[label]}
